Communication between\n28:   the processes takes place only using unix domain sockets.\n29: * An example restarter/parent process written in Python is included in the source distribution at\n30:   :repo:`restarter/hot-restarter.py <restarter/hot-restarter.py>`.\n31:   This parent process is usable with standard process control utilities such as monit/runit/etc.\n32: ","endLine":32,"startLine":25},{"content":"51: By default, Envoy uses :ref:`reuse_port\n52: <envoy_v3_api_field_config.listener.v3.Listener.enable_reuse_port>` sockets on Linux for better\n53: performance. mechanism in v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple C++ source files that handle the coordinated shutdown of the parent process and startup of the child process.\\n\\n**Core Interface (envoy/server/hot_restart.h)** defines the HotRestart abstract base class that provides the public API for hot restart functionality, including methods like drainParentListeners(), duplicateParentListenSocket(), registerUdpForwardingListener(), and parentDrainedCallbackRegistrar(). It also defines HotRestartDomainSocketInUseException for socket binding errors.\\n\\n**Main Implementation (source/server/)** provides three key implementation components:\\n\\n1. **HotRestartImpl** (hot_restart_impl.h/cc) - The main implementation that coordinates parent and child processes. It creates shared memory via attachSharedMemory(), initializes HotRestartingChild and HotRestartingParent instances, and delegates operations to them. The class maintains the base_id and restart_epoch needed for socket naming.\\n\\n2. **HotRestartingBase** (hot_restarting_base.h/cc) - The base class for both parent and child processes that handles RPC communication via Unix domain sockets. It contains the RpcStream class which manages sending and receiving HotRestartMessage protobufs over datagram sockets. Key methods include: sendHotRestartMessage() for transmitting messages with file descriptor passing support, receiveHotRestartMessage() for receiving messages, bindDomainSocket() for establishing Unix domain socket communication endpoints, and getPassedFdIfPresent() for extracting file descriptors from control data.\\n\\n3. **HotRestartingParent** (hot_restarting_parent.h/cc) - Implements parent process logic. The HotRestartingParent::Internal class handles requests from child processes including getListenSocketsForChild() which duplicates listen socket FDs to the child and exportStatsToChild() which sends parent statistics (counters, gauges, and dynamic stat name mappings) to the child.\\n\\n4. **HotRestartingChild** (hot_restarting_child.h/cc) - Implements child process logic. Key methods include: duplicateParentListenSocket() which requests socket FDs from parent, drainParentListeners() which initiates the parent drain sequence, getParentStats() which retrieves parent statistics, and mergeParentStats() which incorporates parent stats into the child's store. The child also implements Network::ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar for registering callbacks when parent draining completes.\\n\\n5. **HotRestartNopImpl** (hot_restart_nop_impl.h) - A no-op implementation used when hot restart is disabled.\\n\\n**Protocol Definition (source/server/hot_restart.proto)** defines the HotRestartMessage protobuf format for parent-child communication. Child->parent requests include PassListenSocket (requesting socket FD), ShutdownAdmin, Stats, DrainListeners, Terminate, ForwardedUdpPacket (for QUIC UDP forwarding), and TestConnection. Parent->child replies provide matching response messages with FD data or stats information.\\n\\n**OS-Specific Implementation (source/common/api/posix/)** provides HotRestartOsSysCallsImpl (os_sys_calls_impl_hot_restart.h/cc) which wraps POSIX system calls for shared memory operations (shmOpen, shmUnlink, mmap) needed for the IPC mechanisms.\\n\\n**Entry Points** - main_common.cc uses hotRestartVersion() to report restart capability, and stripped_main_base.cc initializes HotRestartImpl during server startup, catching HotRestartDomainSocketInUseException and retrying with different base IDs on failure.\\n\\n**Test Files** validate the implementation with comprehensive test coverage including hot_restart_impl_test.cc for integration testing, hot_restarting_parent_test.cc and hot_restarting_child_test.cc for parent/child protocol validation, hot_restarting_base_test.cc for RPC stream functionality, and integration test hotrestart_test.sh for end-to-end scenarios.   }\n   242→  ],\n   243→  \"text\": \"The Envoy hot restart mechanism in v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple C++ source files that handle the coordinated shutdown of the parent process and startup of the child process.\\n\\n**Core Interface (envoy/server/hot_restart.h)** defines the HotRestart abstract base class that provides the public API for hot restart functionality, including methods like drainParentListeners(), duplicateParentListenSocket(), registerUdpForwardingListener(), and parentDrainedCallbackRegistrar(). It also defines HotRestartDomainSocketInUseException for socket binding errors.\\n\\n**Main Implementation (source/server/)** provides three key implementation components:\\n\\n1. **HotRestartImpl** (hot_restart_impl.h/cc) - The main implementation that coordinates parent and child processes. It creates shared memory via attachSharedMemory(), initializes HotRestartingChild and HotRestartingParent instances, and delegates operations to them. The class maintains the base_id and restart_epoch needed for socket naming.\\n\\n2. **HotRestartingBase** (hot_restarting_base.h/cc) - The base class for both parent and child processes that handles RPC communication via Unix domain sockets. It contains the RpcStream class which manages sending and receiving HotRestartMessage protobufs over datagram sockets. Key methods include: sendHotRestartMessage() for transmitting messages with file descriptor passing support, receiveHotRestartMessage() for receiving messages, bindDomainSocket() for establishing Unix domain socket communication endpoints, and getPassedFdIfPresent() for extracting file descriptors from control data.\\n\\n3. **HotRestartingParent** (hot_restarting_parent.h/cc) - Implements parent process logic. The HotRestartingParent::Internal class handles requests from child processes including getListenSocketsForChild() which duplicates listen socket FDs to the child and exportStatsToChild() which sends parent statistics (counters, gauges, and dynamic stat name mappings) to the child.\\n\\n4. **HotRestartingChild** (hot_restarting_child.h/cc) - Implements child process logic. Key methods include: duplicateParentListenSocket() which requests socket FDs from parent, drainParentListeners() which initiates the parent drain sequence, getParentStats() which retrieves parent statistics, and mergeParentStats() which incorporates parent stats into the child's store. The child also implements Network::ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar for registering callbacks when parent draining completes.\\n\\n5. **HotRestartNopImpl** (hot_restart_nop_impl.h) - A no-op implementation used when hot restart is disabled.\\n\\n**Protocol Definition (source/server/hot_restart.proto)** defines the HotRestartMessage protobuf format for parent-child communication. Child->parent requests include PassListenSocket (requesting socket FD), ShutdownAdmin, Stats, DrainListeners, Terminate, ForwardedUdpPacket (for QUIC UDP forwarding), and TestConnection. Parent->child replies provide matching response messages with FD data or stats information.\\n\\n**OS-Specific Implementation (source/common/api/posix/)** provides HotRestartOsSysCallsImpl (os_sys_calls_impl_hot_restart.h/cc) which wraps POSIX system calls for shared memory operations (shmOpen, shmUnlink, mmap) needed for the IPC mechanisms.\\n\\n**Entry Points** - main_common.cc uses hotRestartVersion() to report restart capability, and stripped_main_base.cc initializes HotRestartImpl during server startup, catching HotRestartDomainSocketInUseException and retrying with different base IDs on failure.\\n\\n**Test Files** validate the implementation with comprehensive test coverage including hot_restart_impl_test.cc for integration testing, hot_restarting_parent_test.cc and hot_restarting_child_test.cc for parent/child protocol validation, hot_restarting_base_test.cc for RPC stream functionality, and integration test hotrestart_test.sh for end-to-end scenarios. Mocks are provided in test/mocks/ for testing server components that depend on hot restart.\"\n   244→}\n   245→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. mechanism in v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple C++ source files that handle the coordinated shutdown of the parent process and startup of the child process.\\n\\n**Core Interface (envoy/server/hot_restart.h)** defines the HotRestart abstract base class that provides the public API for hot restart functionality, including methods like drainParentListeners(), duplicateParentListenSocket(), registerUdpForwardingListener(), and parentDrainedCallbackRegistrar(). It also defines HotRestartDomainSocketInUseException for socket binding errors.\\n\\n**Main Implementation (source/server/)** provides three key implementation components:\\n\\n1. **HotRestartImpl** (hot_restart_impl.h/cc) - The main implementation that coordinates parent and child processes. It creates shared memory via attachSharedMemory(), initializes HotRestartingChild and HotRestartingParent instances, and delegates operations to them. The class maintains the base_id and restart_epoch needed for socket naming.\\n\\n2. **HotRestartingBase** (hot_restarting_base.h/cc) - The base class for both parent and child processes that handles RPC communication via Unix domain sockets. It contains the RpcStream class which manages sending and receiving HotRestartMessage protobufs over datagram sockets. Key methods include: sendHotRestartMessage() for transmitting messages with file descriptor passing support, receiveHotRestartMessage() for receiving messages, bindDomainSocket() for establishing Unix domain socket communication endpoints, and getPassedFdIfPresent() for extracting file descriptors from control data.\\n\\n3. **HotRestartingParent** (hot_restarting_parent.h/cc) - Implements parent process logic. The HotRestartingParent::Internal class handles requests from child processes including getListenSocketsForChild() which duplicates listen socket FDs to the child and exportStatsToChild() which sends parent statistics (counters, gauges, and dynamic stat name mappings) to the child.\\n\\n4. **HotRestartingChild** (hot_restarting_child.h/cc) - Implements child process logic. Key methods include: duplicateParentListenSocket() which requests socket FDs from parent, drainParentListeners() which initiates the parent drain sequence, getParentStats() which retrieves parent statistics, and mergeParentStats() which incorporates parent stats into the child's store. The child also implements Network::ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar for registering callbacks when parent draining completes.\\n\\n5. **HotRestartNopImpl** (hot_restart_nop_impl.h) - A no-op implementation used when hot restart is disabled.\\n\\n**Protocol Definition (source/server/hot_restart.proto)** defines the HotRestartMessage protobuf format for parent-child communication. Child->parent requests include PassListenSocket (requesting socket FD), ShutdownAdmin, Stats, DrainListeners, Terminate, ForwardedUdpPacket (for QUIC UDP forwarding), and TestConnection. Parent->child replies provide matching response messages with FD data or stats information.\\n\\n**OS-Specific Implementation (source/common/api/posix/)** provides HotRestartOsSysCallsImpl (os_sys_calls_impl_hot_restart.h/cc) which wraps POSIX system calls for shared memory operations (shmOpen, shmUnlink, mmap) needed for the IPC mechanisms.\\n\\n**Entry Points** - main_common.cc uses hotRestartVersion() to report restart capability, and stripped_main_base.cc initializes HotRestartImpl during server startup, catching HotRestartDomainSocketInUseException and retrying with different base IDs on failure.\\n\\n**Test Files** validate the implementation with comprehensive test coverage including hot_restart_impl_test.cc for integration testing, hot_restarting_parent_test.cc and hot_restarting_child_test.cc for parent/child protocol validation, hot_restarting_base_test.cc for RPC stream functionality, and integration test hotrestart_test.sh for end-to-end scenarios.
